### [296] [HistoFID- Calibrating Frechet-distance evaluation across pathology foundation models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20584)
*Swapnil Bhat,Devansh Lalwani,Maulik Shah,Sheena Alphones,Rimlee Dutta,Nikita Mulchandani,Roshani Gala,Jay Mehta*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了病理图像生成模型中Frechet距离受编码器选择的影响，发现原始分数因编码器不同可变化30倍；提出以编码器自身基线比标准化，使变异系数降低约89%；不同编码器对生成模型的评判结论可能相反，揭示了编码器选择对评估结果的决定性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字病理学中常用组织学基础模型替代Inception网络计算FID，但编码器选择如何影响评估结果尚不清楚，可能导致生成模型比较结论错误。

Method: 使用六种常见编码器（Inception-v3、Phikon-v2、CONCH、UNI2-h、Virchow2、Prov-GigaPath）在约50万张HE和免疫组化切片上进行实验，测量不同编码器下的Frechet距离，并提出标准化比率方法。

Result: 同一对切片的原始Frechet距离跨编码器变化约30倍；标准化比率使跨编码器变异系数降低约89%（同队列）和58%（跨队列）；编码器分为敏感组和不变组，两组对生成模型的优劣评判结论相反。

Conclusion: 编码器选择从根本上影响病理图像评估结果，报告FID时必须注明所用编码器；所提出的标准化方案可恢复跨编码器的可比性。

Abstract: The Frechet Inception Distance (FID) compares two image sets by fitting a Gaussian to the features of a fixed network and measuring the distance between the two Gaussians. In digital pathology the Inception network is routinely replaced by a histology foundation model, on the assumption that a domain encoder gives a more meaningful score. We show that this choice changes the result. For one fixed pair of tile sets, the raw Frechet distance varies about thirty-fold across six common encoders, and the ordering does not follow embedding dimension, so a raw score cannot be read without naming the encoder. Using a held-out in-house cohort (about 500,000 H&E and immunohistochemistry tiles from 2,119 slides) and a public TCGA BRCA cohort (100 slides), we benchmark Inception-v3, Phikon-v2, CONCH, UNI2-h, Virchow2 and Prov-GigaPath across within-cohort baselines, cross-cohort drift, controlled perturbations, compression, stain normalization, and two generative models. Expressing each distance as a ratio to the encoder's own within-cohort floor restores comparability, cutting the across-encoder coefficient of variation by about 89% within cohort and 58% across cohorts. The encoders separate into a sensitive group (CONCH, Phikon-v2, Inception-v3) and an invariant group (UNI2-h, Virchow2, Prov-GigaPath), and this split decides which generative model is judged more realistic, so the encoder can change the conclusion of a generative evaluation. At the slide level, an attention-pooling encoder registers per-slide composition that a pooled patch distance cannot see, raising the distance about 320-fold on matched cohorts. Using the same protocol we evaluate TuroCompress, a proprietary pathology codec, which reaches the highest reconstruction fidelity at the smallest file size among codecs tested. We release the normalization protocol, the per-encoder perturbation panel, and the feature extracts.

</details>


### [297] [MedDiT4SR: Tri-Stream Joint Adaptation of Pre-Trained Diffusion Transformers for Medical Image Super-Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20598)
*Zhi Chen,Le Zhang*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 提出MedDiT4SR，一种三流适配框架，将预训练的多模态扩散Transformer适配到医学图像超分辨率，通过三流集成、SR适配器和语义对齐精炼器实现高质量重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ControlNet式适配中，低分辨率图像作为外部条件单向注入去噪流，导致低分辨率解剖证据无法与不断演化的去噪和语义表示联合更新，限制了预训练多模态扩散Transformer在医学图像超分辨率中的有效性。

Method: 提出MedDiT4SR三流适配框架：(1) 将低分辨率、噪声潜变量和文本表示集成到同一多模态扩散Transformer块中；(2) 引入SR适配器，聚合尺度相关的局部token并抑制插值引入的冗余；(3) 提出语义对齐精炼器，利用提示条件语义信息校准局部低分辨率响应。

Result: 在域内和跨数据集设置下的实验表明，该方法能有效将大规模预训练DiT模型适配到不同成像领域的医学图像超分辨率任务中。

Conclusion: MedDiT4SR通过三流联合更新机制和双重适配模块，成功克服了传统单向适配的局限，为预训练大模型在医学图像超分辨率中的应用提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Medical image super-resolution (MedSR) requires recovering fine anatomical structures from degraded observations while avoiding unsupported details introduced by generative priors. Large-scale pre-trained multimodal diffusion transformers provide strong visual priors, but their adaptation to MedSR remains non-trivial. In conventional ControlNet-style adaptation, the low-resolution (LR) image is processed as an external condition and injected into the denoising stream through one-way connections. Consequently, LR anatomical evidence cannot be jointly updated with the evolving denoising and semantic representations. We propose MedDiT4SR, a tri-stream adaptation framework that integrates the LR, noisy latent, and text representations into the same multimodal diffusion-transformer blocks. To complement global token interaction, we introduce a Super-Resolution Adapter (SR Adapter) that aggregates scale-dependent local tokens and suppresses interpolation-induced redundancy. We further propose a Semantic Alignment Refiner (SA Refiner) that calibrates local LR responses using prompt-conditioned semantic information. Experiments under both in-domain and within-modality cross-dataset settings demonstrate the effectiveness of adapting large-scale pre-trained DiT models to medical image super-resolution across diverse imaging domains.

</details>


### [298] [From Attention to Frequency: Integration of Vision Transformer and FFT-ReLU for Enhanced Image Deblurring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10806)
*Syed Mumtahin Mahmud,Mahdi Mohd Hossain Noki,Prothito Shovon Majumder,Abdul Mohaimen Al Radi,Md. Haider Ali,Md. Mosaddek Khan*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 提出了一种统一视觉Transformer与频域FFT-ReLU模块的双域架构，用于图像去模糊，在多个基准数据集上取得了优于现有方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法（如CNN和ViT）在处理复杂或高分辨率模糊时计算开销大且效果有限，需要一种更高效且能保留细节的去模糊方法。

Method: 提出双域架构：ViT主干网络建模空间局部与全局依赖，FFT-ReLU模块在频域施加稀疏约束以抑制模糊伪影并保留细节。

Result: 在基准数据集上，该方法在PSNR、SSIM和感知质量上均优于现有最先进模型，定量指标、定性对比和人工偏好评估均验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法为实际图像恢复任务建立了一个实用且可泛化的范式，证明了空间-频域联合建模的有效性。

Abstract: Image deblurring is vital in computer vision, aiming to recover sharp images from blurry ones caused by motion or camera shake. While deep learning approaches such as CNNs and Vision Transformers (ViTs) have advanced this field, they often struggle with complex or high-resolution blur and computational demands. We propose a new dual-domain architecture that unifies Vision Transformers with a frequency-domain FFT-ReLU module, explicitly bridging spatial attention modeling and frequency sparsity. In this structure, the ViT backbone captures local and global dependencies, while the FFT-ReLU component enforces frequency-domain sparsity to suppress blur-related artifacts and preserve fine details. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets demonstrate that this architecture achieves superior PSNR, SSIM, and perceptual quality compared to state-of-the-art models. Both quantitative metrics, qualitative comparisons, and human preference evaluations confirm its effectiveness, establishing a practical and generalizable paradigm for real-world image restoration.

</details>
